<h3 id="range" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#range"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Range</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can add multiple thumbs to the slider by adding multiple <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Slider.Thumb</code></p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="marks" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#marks"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Marks</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can add marks to the slider track by using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Slider.MarkerGroup</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Slider.Marker</code> components.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Position the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Slider.Marker</code> components relative to the track by providing the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> prop.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8phanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="min-and-max" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#min-and-max"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Min and Max</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">By default, the minimum is <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">0</code> and the maximum is <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">100</code>. If that&#x27;s not what you want, you can easily specify different
bounds by changing the values of the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">min</code> and/or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">max</code> props.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">For example, to ask the user for a value between <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">-10</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">10</code>, you can use:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_91hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_91hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_91hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="granularity" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#granularity"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Granularity</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">By default, the granularity, is <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">1</code>, meaning that the value is always an integer. You can change the step attribute to
control the granularity.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">For example, If you need a value between <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">5</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">10</code>, accurate to two decimal places, you should set the value of step
to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">0.01</code>:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_99hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="change-events" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#change-events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Change Events</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">When the slider value changes, the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChangeEnd</code> callbacks are invoked. You can use this to set
up custom behaviors in your app.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="orientation" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#orientation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Orientation</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">By default, the slider is assumed to be horizontal. To change the orientation to vertical, set the orientation property
in the machine&#x27;s context to vertical.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">In this mode, the slider will use the arrow up and down keys to increment/decrement its value.</p>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Don&#x27;t forget to change the styles of the vertical slider by specifying its height</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="origin" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#origin"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Origin</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">By default, the slider&#x27;s origin is at the start of the track. To change the origin to the center of the track, set the
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">origin</code> prop to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">center</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9vhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the slider is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useSlider</code> hook. This way you
can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a5hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a5hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a5hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="dragging-indicator" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#dragging-indicator"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Dragging Indicator</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Slider.DraggingIndicator</code> component inside <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Slider.Thumb</code> to show a visual indicator while the thumb is being
dragged.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_abhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_abhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_abhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="thumb-overlap" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#thumb-overlap"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Thumb Overlap</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">minStepsBetweenThumbs</code> prop to prevent range slider thumbs from overlapping. This ensures a minimum gap between
thumbs, which is useful for price range filters and similar use cases.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_ahhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_ahhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_ahhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="thumb-collision" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#thumb-collision"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Thumb Collision</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">thumbCollisionBehavior</code> prop to control how thumbs behave when they collide during pointer interactions.
Supported values are <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">push</code> (default), <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">swap</code>, and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">none</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_anhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_anhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_anhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>

| &#x27;start&#x27; | &#x27;end&#x27;</code><p class="text">The origin of the slider range. The track is filled from the origin
to the thumb for single values.
- &quot;start&quot;: Useful when the value represents an absolute value

- &quot;end&quot;: Useful when the value represents an offset from the end</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">number</code><p class="text">The step value of the slider</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">thumbAlignment</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&#x27;contain&#x27;</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&#x27;center&#x27; | &#x27;contain&#x27;</code><p class="text">The alignment of the slider thumb relative to the track
- `center`: the thumb will extend beyond the bounds of the slider track.
- `contain`: the thumb will be contained within the bounds of the track.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">thumbCollisionBehavior</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&#x27;none&#x27;</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&#x27;none&#x27; | &#x27;push&#x27; | &#x27;swap&#x27;</code><p class="text">Controls how thumbs behave when they collide during pointer interactions.
- `none` (default): Thumbs cannot move past each other; excess movement is ignored.
- `push`: Thumbs push each other without restoring their previous positions when dragged back.
- `swap`: Thumbs swap places when dragged past each other.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">thumbSize</code></td><td class="w_28 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-minus icon icon--size_xs c_fg.muted" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M5 12h14"></path></svg></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">{ width: number; height: number }</code><p class="text">The slider thumbs dimensions</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(index: number) =&gt; void</code><p class="text">Function to increment the value of the slider at the given index.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">decrement</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(index: number) =&gt; void</code><p class="text">Function to decrement the value of the slider at the given index.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">focus</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">VoidFunction</code><p class="text">Function to focus the slider. This focuses the first thumb.</p></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Complies with the <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/slider/" class="link">Slider WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>

Range\n\nYou can add multiple thumbs to the slider by adding multiple `Slider.Thumb`\n\n**Example: range**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/react/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const Range = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root defaultValue={[30, 60]} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track className={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range className={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={1} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/solid/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const Range = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root defaultValue={[30, 60]} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={1} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/vue/slider'\nimport styles from \u003cSlider.Range :class=\"styles.Range\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"0\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"1\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Slider } from '@ark-ui/svelte/slider'\n Marks\n\nYou can add marks to the slider track by using the `Slider.MarkerGroup` and `Slider.Marker` components.\n\nPosition the `Slider.Marker` components relative to the track by providing the `value` prop.\n\n**Example: with-marks**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/react/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const WithMarks = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue={[50]}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText className={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track className={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range className={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.MarkerGroup className={styles.MarkerGroup}\u003e\n        {[0, 25, 50, 75, 100].map((value) =\u003e (\n          \u003cSlider.Marker key={value} value={value} className={styles.Marker}\u003e\n            {value}\n          \u003c/Slider.Marker\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/Slider.MarkerGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/solid/slider'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const WithMarks = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={[50]}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', 'justify-content': 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.MarkerGroup class={styles.MarkerGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cFor each={[0, 25, 50, 75, 100]}\u003e\n          {(value) =\u003e (\n            \u003cSlider.Marker value={value} class={styles.Marker}\u003e\n              {value}\n            \u003c/Slider.Marker\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/For\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.MarkerGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/vue/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nconst marks = [0, 25, 50, 75, 100]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :default-value=\"[50]\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :style=\"{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.ValueText :class=\"styles.ValueText\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Track :class=\"styles.Track\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Range :class=\"styles.Range\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"0\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.MarkerGroup :class=\"styles.MarkerGroup\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Marker v-for=\"value in marks\" :key=\"value\" :value=\"value\" :class=\"styles.Marker\"\u003e\n        {{ value }}\n      \u003c/Slider.Marker\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.MarkerGroup\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Slider } from '@ark-ui/svelte/slider'\n  import styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\n  const marks = [0, 25, 50, 75, 100]\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSlider.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={[50]}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; justify-content: space-between;\"\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.MarkerGroup class={styles.MarkerGroup}\u003e\n    {#each marks as value}\n      \u003cSlider.Marker {value} class={styles.Marker}\u003e{value}\u003c/Slider.Marker\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/Slider.MarkerGroup\u003e\n\u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Min and Max\n\nBy default, the minimum is `0` and the maximum is `100`. If that's not what you want, you can easily specify different\nbounds by changing the values of the `min` and/or `max` props.\n\nFor example, to ask the user for a value between `-10` and `10`, you can use:\n\n**Example: min-max**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/react/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const MinMax = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root min={-10} max={10} defaultValue={[5]} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText className={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track className={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range className={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/solid/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const MinMax = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root min={-10} max={10} defaultValue={[5]} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', 'justify-content': 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/vue/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Root :min=\"-10\" :max=\"10\" :default-value=\"[5]\" :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :style=\"{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.ValueText :class=\"styles.ValueText\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Track :class=\"styles.Track\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Range :class=\"styles.Range\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"0\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Slider } from '@ark-ui/svelte/slider'\n  import styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSlider.Root min={-10} max={10} defaultValue={[5]} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; justify-content: space-between;\"\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Granularity\n\nBy default, the granularity, is `1`, meaning that the value is always an integer. You can change the step attribute to\ncontrol the granularity.\n\nFor example, If you need a value between `5` and `10`, accurate to two decimal places, you should set the value of step\nto `0.01`:\n\n**Example: step**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/react/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const Step = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root step={0.01} min={5} max={10} defaultValue={[7.5]} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText className={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track className={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range className={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/solid/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const Step = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root step={0.01} min={5} max={10} defaultValue={[7.5]} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', 'justify-content': 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/vue/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Root :step=\"0.01\" :min=\"5\" :max=\"10\" :default-value=\"[7.5]\" :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :style=\"{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.ValueText :class=\"styles.ValueText\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Track :class=\"styles.Track\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Range :class=\"styles.Range\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"0\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Slider } from '@ark-ui/svelte/slider'\n  import styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSlider.Root step={0.01} min={5} max={10} defaultValue={[7.5]} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; justify-content: space-between;\"\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Change Events\n\nWhen the slider value changes, the `onValueChange` and `onValueChangeEnd` callbacks are invoked. You can use this to set\nup custom behaviors in your app.\n\n**Example: on-event**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/react/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const OnEvent = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root\n      onValueChange={(details) =\u003e console.log('onValueChange', details.value)}\n      onValueChangeEnd={(details) =\u003e console.log('onValueChangeEnd', details.value)}\n      className={styles.Root}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText className={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track className={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range className={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/solid/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const OnEvent = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root\n      onValueChange={(details) =\u003e console.log('onValueChange', details.value)}\n      onValueChangeEnd={(details) =\u003e console.log('onValueChangeEnd', details.value)}\n      class={styles.Root}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', 'justify-content': 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/vue/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Root\n    :class=\"styles.Root\"\n    @value-change=\"(details) =\u003e console.log('onValueChange', details.value)\"\n    @value-change-end=\"(details) =\u003e console.log('onValueChangeEnd', details.value)\"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cdiv :style=\"{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.ValueText :class=\"styles.ValueText\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Track :class=\"styles.Track\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Range :class=\"styles.Range\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"0\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Slider, type SliderValueChangeDetails } from '@ark-ui/svelte/slider'\n  import styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\n  const handleValueChange = (details: SliderValueChangeDetails) =\u003e {\n    console.log('onValueChange', details.value)\n  }\n\n  const handleValueChangeEnd = (details: SliderValueChangeDetails) =\u003e {\n    console.log('onValueChangeEnd', details.value)\n  }\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSlider.Root class={styles.Root} onValueChange={handleValueChange} onValueChangeEnd={handleValueChangeEnd}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; justify-content: space-between;\"\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Orientation\n\nBy default, the slider is assumed to be horizontal. To change the orientation to vertical, set the orientation property\nin the machine's context to vertical.\n\nIn this mode, the slider will use the arrow up and down keys to increment/decrement its value.\n\n\u003e Don't forget to change the styles of the vertical slider by specifying its height\n\n**Example: vertical**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/react/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const Vertical = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root orientation=\"vertical\" className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.ValueText className={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track className={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range className={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/solid/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const Vertical = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root orientation=\"vertical\" class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/vue/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Root orientation=\"vertical\" :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.ValueText :class=\"styles.ValueText\" /\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Track :class=\"styles.Track\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Range :class=\"styles.Range\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"0\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Slider } from '@ark-ui/svelte/slider'\n  import styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSlider.Root orientation=\"vertical\" class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Origin\n\nBy default, the slider's origin is at the start of the track. To change the origin to the center of the track, set the\n`origin` prop to `center`.\n\n**Example: center-origin**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/react/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const CenterOrigin = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root origin=\"center\" className={styles.Root} defaultValue={[75]}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText className={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track className={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range className={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/solid/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const CenterOrigin = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root origin=\"center\" class={styles.Root} defaultValue={[75]}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', 'justify-content': 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/vue/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Root origin=\"center\" :class=\"styles.Root\" :default-value=\"[75]\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :style=\"{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.ValueText :class=\"styles.ValueText\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Track :class=\"styles.Track\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Range :class=\"styles.Range\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"0\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Slider } from '@ark-ui/svelte/slider'\n  import styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSlider.Root origin=\"center\" class={styles.Root} defaultValue={[75]}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; justify-content: space-between;\"\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the slider is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useSlider` hook. This way you\ncan access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider, useSlider } from '@ark-ui/react/slider'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const slider = useSlider()\n\n  return (\n    \u003c\u003e\n      \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e slider.focus()}\u003e\n        Focus\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cSlider.RootProvider value={slider} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText className={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Track className={styles.Track}\u003e\n            \u003cSlider.Range className={styles.Range} /\u003e\n          \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n            \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n          \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider, useSlider } from '@ark-ui/solid/slider'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const slider = useSlider()\n\n  return (\n    \u003c\u003e\n      \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e slider().focus()}\u003e\n        Focus\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cSlider.RootProvider value={slider} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n            \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n          \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n            \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n          \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Slider, useSlider } from '@ark-ui/vue/slider'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nconst slider = useSlider()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"slider.focus()\"\u003eFocus\u003c/button\u003e\n\n  \u003cSlider.RootProvider :value=\"slider\" :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.ValueText :class=\"styles.ValueText\" /\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Track :class=\"styles.Track\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Range :class=\"styles.Range\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"0\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Slider, useSlider } from '@ark-ui/svelte/slider'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const slider = useSlider({ id })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cbutton class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e slider().focus()}\u003eFocus\u003c/button\u003e\n\n\u003cSlider.RootProvider value={slider} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Slider.RootProvider\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Dragging Indicator\n\nUse the `Slider.DraggingIndicator` component inside `Slider.Thumb` to show a visual indicator while the thumb is being\ndragged.\n\n**Example: dragging-indicator**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/react/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const DraggingIndicator = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue={[40]}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track className={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range className={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.DraggingIndicator className={styles.DraggingIndicator} /\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/solid/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const DraggingIndicator = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={[40]}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.DraggingIndicator class={styles.DraggingIndicator} /\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/vue/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :default-value=\"[40]\"\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Track :class=\"styles.Track\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Range :class=\"styles.Range\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"0\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.DraggingIndicator :class=\"styles.DraggingIndicator\" /\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Slider } from '@ark-ui/svelte/slider'\n  import styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSlider.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={[40]}\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.DraggingIndicator class={styles.DraggingIndicator} /\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Thumb Overlap\n\nUse the `minStepsBetweenThumbs` prop to prevent range slider thumbs from overlapping. This ensures a minimum gap between\nthumbs, which is useful for price range filters and similar use cases.\n\n**Example: thumb-overlap**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/react/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const ThumbOverlap = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root minStepsBetweenThumbs={5} defaultValue={[25, 60]} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText className={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track className={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range className={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={1} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/solid/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const ThumbOverlap = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root minStepsBetweenThumbs={5} defaultValue={[25, 60]} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', 'justify-content': 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"0\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"1\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Thumb index={1} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n\u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Thumb Collision\n\nUse the `thumbCollisionBehavior` prop to control how thumbs behave when they collide during pointer interactions.\nSupported values are `push` (default), `swap`, and `none`.\n\n**Example: thumb-collision**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/react/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const ThumbCollision = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root thumbCollisionBehavior=\"push\" defaultValue={[25, 60]} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText className={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track className={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range className={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={1} className={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/solid/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\nexport const ThumbCollision = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cSlider.Root thumbCollisionBehavior=\"push\" defaultValue={[25, 60]} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', 'justify-content': 'space-between' }}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Track class={styles.Track}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.Range class={styles.Range} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={0} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Thumb index={1} class={styles.Thumb}\u003e\n          \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Slider } from '@ark-ui/vue/slider'\nimport styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSlider.Root thumb-collision-behavior=\"push\" :default-value=\"[25, 60]\" :class=\"styles.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cdiv :style=\"{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.ValueText :class=\"styles.ValueText\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Track :class=\"styles.Track\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.Range :class=\"styles.Range\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Track\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"0\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n      \u003cSlider.Thumb :index=\"1\" :class=\"styles.Thumb\"\u003e\n        \u003cSlider.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/Slider.Thumb\u003e\n    \u003c/Slider.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/Slider.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Slider } from '@ark-ui/svelte/slider'\n  import styles from 'styles/slider.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSlider.Root thumbCollisionBehavior=\"push\" defaultValue={[25, 60]} class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cdiv style=\"display: flex; justify-content: space-between;\"\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/Slider.Label\u003e\n    \u003cSlider.ValueText class={styles.ValueText} /\u003e\n
